Arrived at the hotel in the afternoon, and just entered the room, I found that the windows were covered with bugs, the bugs that looked like Mrs. Smelly, there were about ten of them, crawling everywhere on the windows, curtains, and walls. I called the front desk, and the waitress came to help me catch bugs. I wanted to change rooms, but the older sister said that any room is the same, and the screens are not closed tightly, and the bugs will crawl in. The older sister came back twice, and caught more than a dozen in total. Only, we closed the windows for fear of crawling into the insects again, and then the problem came again. The weather was very hot, more than 20 degrees, and the sun made the house even hotter. The thermometer showed 28 degrees, and the air conditioner did not cool down. I called the front desk and the front desk said that the air conditioner had stopped, and now we can only blow natural wind. The temperature in the room did not drop until we checked out the next day.
The seafood buffet at the hotel at night may be due to the fact that there are few people now, and some dishes are not very fresh. The meat of the particularly large shrimp is scattered, and it will be bad if you touch it lightly. You canâ€™t eat it. Abalone is the best, live Fresh, the crabs were supposed to be alive, but after a long time of picking, only one that could move was picked, and the others were motionless. I was afraid they were dead crabs, so I didn't dare to eat them. The cakes were placed at the door, and many of them looked dry, apparently for a long time.
The buffet breakfast on the second day was probably due to the fact that there were no people, and there were few dishes. Some sausages tasted delicious, and the fruits seemed to be leftover from the night before. This is the self-service that sells 99 people, and I have learned a lot.
Originally, we planned to check out at noon, but as soon as the sun came out in the morning, a dozen or so bugs crawled in. I was so scared that I checked out cleanly. I went down and told the front desk that the front desk did not apologize but it was due to a seasonal problem , although there are many insects in this season, if the hotel windows are better, can the insects still crawl in?
I chose to stay after reading the reviews and thought it was very good, but after staying for one night, I really feel that the hotel is ruining my reputation. I have stayed in many holidays at home and abroad, and this is the first time I have encountered such a situation. The picture is of bugs, I really dare not get close, I took a few pictures from a distance, and many of them were behind the curtains.
